<script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
        var searchIcon = $('#searchIcon');
        var searchIconSrc = searchIcon.attr('src');
        var closeIconSrc = "https://www.ppatour.com/wp-content/themes/ppa-tour_08-06-2025/assets/media/svg/icon-close.svg";

        // Toggle the search modal, icon, and active class on click of the search icon
        searchIcon.click(function() {
            $('.header__search-form').toggle();
            $('.header__search').toggleClass('active');
            $('#header-container').toggleClass('search-active'); // Toggle class for #headerContainer

            // Check if the search form is visible
            if ($('.header__search-form').is(':visible')) {
                // Change icon to close icon
                searchIcon.attr('src', closeIconSrc);
            } else {
                // Change icon back to search icon
                searchIcon.attr('src', searchIconSrc);
            }
        });

        // Close the search modal and remove active class on click of the close icon
        $('.header__search-form-content-close').click(function() {
            $('.header__search-form').hide();
            $('.header__search').removeClass('active');
            $('#header-container').removeClass('search-active'); // Remove class from #headerContainer
            // Change icon back to search icon
            searchIcon.attr('src', searchIconSrc);
        });
    });
</script>

                                                            <h4 class="tickets__content-heading typo-heading typo-heading--4">Ground Pass</h3>
                            
                                                            <div class="tickets__content-text typo-body typo-body--medium"><p>A Grounds Pass gives you access to every amateur and professional match that is <strong>NOT</strong> played on Humana Championship Court. Matches are assigned to courts in real-time during the tournament based on court availability. You can find each court assignment by following the bracket on our website each day of the tournament.</p>
</div>

                                                            <h4 class="tickets__content-heading typo-heading typo-heading--4">CIBC VIP Ticket</h3>
                            
                                                            <div class="tickets__content-text typo-body typo-body--medium"><p>Like a Courtside Pass, CIBC VIP Tickets give you access to all amateur and professional matches, including matches played on Humana Championship Court. However, a CIBC VIP Ticket also comes with catered lunch, snacks, stocked coolers with cold drinks (including alcohol), and exclusive access to the CIBC VIP lounge. CIBC VIP seating on Humana Championship Court is on chairs and is organized on a first-come, first-serve basis.</p>
</div>

			<div class="col-lg-6 col-12 tournament-single__venue-details">
				<div class="tournament-single__venue-col-wrapper">
					<h3 class="typo-heading typo-heading--3">The Las Vegas Convention Center</h3>
					<p class="typo-heading">The Las Vegas Convention Center, 3150 Paradise Rd, Las Vegas, NV 89109</p>
											<p>Operated by the Las Vegas Convention and Visitors Authority (LVCVA), the Las Vegas Convention Center is one of the busiest facilities in the world &#8211; a 4.6 million-square-foot facility located within a short distance to 150,000 hotel rooms. Well known for its versatility with approximately 2.9 million square feet of exhibit space, 225 meeting rooms (more than 390,000 square feet) and seating capacities ranging from 20 to 2,500. Two grand lobby and registration areas, one located in the West Hall, and the other in Central Hall (more than 260,000 square feet) efficiently link existing exhibit halls with new exhibit and meeting rooms, and allow simultaneous set-up, break-down and exhibiting of multiple events.</p>
										<div class="tournament-single__venue-buttons">
													<a class="button button--primary-yellow" href="https://maps.app.goo.gl/QYNzdSYbqTFAmrASA" 
							target="_blank">
							Get Directions							</a>
																			<a class="button button--primary" href="https://www.vegasmeansbusiness.com/meeting-facilities/convention-and-conference-facilities/las-vegas-convention-center/" 
							target="_blank">
							Learn More							</a>
											</div>

				</div>
			</div>

<p style="text-align: left;" data-pm-slice="1 1 []">We recommend parking in the <strong>Bronze Lot</strong>, which is closest to our ticketing entrance at the South Hall (S1). The standard parking fee is $15/day.</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">If the Bronze Lot is full, additional parking is available in other nearby convention center lots.</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">If you’re using <strong>rideshare</strong>, select the S2 entrance for drop-off. Our event entrance is located at S1.</p>
